<plain_text><page sequence="1">Index of Names and Topics Note: Names and topics have been alphabetized following the word-by-word system; for example, "New Zealand" precedes "Newberry." Names with prefixes (De, Van, etc.) are treated as single words; compound names, however, are alphabetized as separate words, so that "Hall-Winters" would precede Hallam. Names beginning with M', Mac, Mc, and St. have been alphabetized as though they were spelled out. Diacriticals have been ignored in alphabetizing. Under a person's name, book titles follow other subtopics. Book reviews are found in a separate index (see Table of Contents).
